### Intro Events ###

country_event = { #Epistles to the Brothers-Agrarians
	id = ukraine_events.2
	title = ukraine_events.2.t
	desc = ukraine_events.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_lypinskyi

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.2 option ukraine_events.2.a"
		name = ukraine_events.2.a
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.2 option ukraine_events.2.b"
		name = ukraine_events.2.b
		country_event = ukraine_events.3
	}
}

### Lead-up to the Revolt ###

country_event = { # Dissent in the West
	id = ukraine_events.11
	title = ukraine_events.11.t
	desc = ukraine_events.11.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_farming

	option = { # Troubling
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.11 option ukraine_events.11.a"
		name = ukraine_events.11.a
		add_stability = -0.01
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_events.12 random_hours = 120 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Tractor Factory Opens In Kyiv
	id = ukraine_events.12
	title = ukraine_events.12.t
	desc = ukraine_events.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_economy_growth
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Great!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.12 option ukraine_events.12.a"
		name = ukraine_events.12.a
		add_political_power = 30
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_events.13 days = 2 } # Strikes In Odesa
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Strikes In Odesa
	id = ukraine_events.13
	title = ukraine_events.13.t
	desc = ukraine_events.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_strike
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukraine_events.14 # Rally in Rivne
				days = 2
				random_hours = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Give empty promises
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.13 option ukraine_events.13.a"
		name = ukraine_events.13.a

		add_political_power = -15
		add_stability = -0.01
	}

	option = { # Send police
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.13 option ukraine_events.13.b"
		name = ukraine_events.13.b

		add_political_power = -5
		add_stability = -0.03
	}
}

country_event = { # Rally in Rivne
	id = ukraine_events.14
	title = ukraine_events.14.t
	desc = ukraine_events.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_syndicalist_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.14 option ukraine_events.14.a"
		name = ukraine_events.14.a #Have Petlyura arrested
		ai_chance = {
			base = 65
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_USKHD_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		custom_effect_tooltip = ukraine_events.14.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_events.15 days = 2 } # Petlyura evades arrest
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.14 option ukraine_events.14.b"
		name = ukraine_events.14.b #Leave Him
		ai_chance = { base = 35 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_petliura_left_alone
	}
}

country_event = { # Black Monday Hits Ukraine!
	id = ukraine_events.16
	title = ukraine_events.16.t
	desc = ukraine_events.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_run_on_the_banks
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # We still have time
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.16 option ukraine_events.16.a"
		name = ukraine_events.16.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_ideas = UKR_black_monday
		set_variable = { UKR_BM_length = 625 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.1 days = 18 } # Start of Relief Bill negotiations
			country_event = { id = ukraine_events.17 days = 60 } # Formation of VDR
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Severity of protests increases in August
	id = ukraine_events.25
	title = ukraine_events.25.t
	desc = {
		text = ukraine_events.25.d1
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_bill_failed }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukraine_events.25.d2
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_bill_successful }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_BEL_Hainaut_Liberated
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.25 option ukraine_events.25.a"
		name = ukraine_events.25.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_bill_failed }	# Bill failed, Soim is seen as unreliable
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_events.26 days = 3 } # SHD approaches Hetman about martial law
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.35 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Appointment of Supreme Otaman
	id = ukraine_events.35
	title = ukraine_events.35.t
	desc = ukraine_events.35.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1

	option = { #prisovskyi
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.35 option ukraine_events.35.a"
		name = ukraine_events.35.a
		trigger = { has_character = UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi }
		UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
	}
	option = { #konovalets
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.35 option ukraine_events.35.b"
		name = ukraine_events.35.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
		}
		UKR_yevhen_konovalets = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
	}
	option = { #Melynk as Konovalets' replacement
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.35 option ukraine_events.35.b2"
		name = ukraine_events.35.b2
		trigger = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
		UKR_andrii_melnyk = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	option = { #ivan p-o
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.35 option ukraine_events.35.c"
		name = ukraine_events.35.c
		trigger = { has_character = UKR_ivan_poltavets_ostrianytsia }
		UKR_ivan_poltavets_ostrianytsia = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
	}
	option = { #zahrodskyi as prisovskyi's replacement
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.35 option ukraine_events.35.e"
		name = ukraine_events.35.e
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character = UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi } }
		UKR_oleksandr_zahrodskyi = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator

		}
	}

country_event = { #Nation at war
	id = ukraine_events.58
	title = ukraine_events.58.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = no
			is_monarchy = yes
			RUS = {
				has_elected_government = yes
				is_monarchy = no
			}
		}
		text = ukraine_events.58.d1 #hetmanate vs democratic RUS
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			RUS = {
				has_elected_government = yes
				is_monarchy = no
			}
		}
		text = ukraine_events.58.d2 #democratic UKR vs democratic RUS
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = no
			is_monarchy = yes
			RUS = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		}
		text = ukraine_events.58.d3 #hetmanate vs socialist RUS
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_socialist_government = yes } }
				OR = {
					has_elected_government = yes
					is_monarchy = no
				}
			}
			else = {
				OR = {
					RUS = { has_elected_government = no }
					RUS = { is_monarchy = yes }
					AND = {
						has_elected_government = no
						is_monarchy = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = ukraine_events.58.d4 #generic
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_war_with = RUS
		NOT = { has_government = syndicalist }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_towar
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = allow_sound_events_flag }
			hidden_effect = { scoped_play_song = ukraine_is_not_yet_lost }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.58 option ukraine_events.58.a"
		name = ukraine_events.58.a
		add_war_support = 0.03
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = UKR_a_family_new_and_free
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = UKR_revbloc_collapse
				}
				has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.166 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
			UKR_oleksii_fedorov = { set_nationality = UKR }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Grain sales improve greatly
	id = ukraine_events.60
	title = ukraine_events.60.t
	desc = ukraine_events.60.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.60 option ukraine_events.60.a"
		name = ukraine_events.60.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = -0.03
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = -0.03
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -5 }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_record_grain_sales
			days = 365
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.60 option ukraine_events.60.b"
		name = ukraine_events.60.b
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 10 }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_monarchy = yes }
				GER = { country_event = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.37 }
			}
		}
	}
}

				rename_state_effect = yes
			}
			200 = {

					set_state_name = VICTORY_POINTS_11405_ZAPORIZHZHIA
					set_province_name = { id = 11405 name = VICTORY_POINTS_11405_ZAPORIZHZHIA }
				}
				rename_state_effect = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {

			}

		add_to_variable = { UKR.UKR_army_land_reinforce_rate = 0.03 }
		UKR_yevhen_konovalets = { add_attack = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi }
			UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_line_break
				add_attack = 1
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_trait = panzer_expert } }
					add_unit_leader_trait = panzer_leader
				}
			}
		}
		UKR_petro_diachenko = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_line_break
			add_attack = 1
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = panzer_expert } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = panzer_leader
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_mastery_bonus = {
			name = UKR_primacy_of_maneuver
			bonus = 0.1
			days = 365
			track = armor
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Army reform event for removing Domestic Bombing Force
	id = ukraine_events.101

		name = ukraine_republican_events.242.a
		add_to_variable = { UKR.UKR_air_attack_factor = 0.1 }

			limit = { has_dlc_bba = yes }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = UKR_fire_from_sky
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = cas_bomber
				category = cat_air_bombs
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = UKR_fire_from_sky
				bonus = 1
				uses = 1
				category = cas_bomber
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_aat = no }
			if = {
				limit = { amount_taken_ideas = { amount > 0 slots = { aircraft_manufacturer } } }
				air_experience = 40
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = anatra
			}
		}
		else = {
			mio:UKR_anatra_organisation = {
				add_mio_size = 1
				add_mio_funds = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	}

# Army Reorg Events (Hetman)

country_event = { # Start of the Relief Bill negotiations
	id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.1
	title = ukraine_relief_bill_events.1.t
	desc = ukraine_relief_bill_events.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference1
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.5 days = 17 random_days = 4 } # USKhD proposes creation of temporary corporate group in the Soim
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_bill_negotiations_flag
		set_variable = { UKR_independents_support = 40 }
		set_variable = { UKR_urdp_support = 30 }
		set_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = 10 }
		set_variable = { UKR_uskhd_support = 40 }
		set_variable = { UKR_udkhp_support = 40 }

		set_variable = { UKR_bm_focuses = 0 }
	}

	option = { # Lets hope for the best
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.1 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.1.a"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_relief_bill_guide_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_protofis target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_URDP target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_udkhp target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_uskhd target = THIS }
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_independents target = THIS }
		}
		else = {
			activate_targeted_decision = { decision = AI_dont_spend_PP target = THIS }
		}
		activate_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
	}
}

country_event = { # URDP proposes temporary nationalization of banking Centres. SHD supports it
	id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.2
	title = ukraine_relief_bill_events.2.t
	desc = ukraine_relief_bill_events.2.d
	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference1
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.9 days = 17 random_days = 4 } # Protofis suggests to keep selling stockpiled grain
		}
	}
	option = { # accept
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.2 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.2.a"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.2.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_urdp }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_urdp_support = 10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_udkhp }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_udkhp_support = 10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_uskhd }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_uskhd_support = 10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_decrease_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_protofis }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = -10 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_promises_to_protofis
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_promises_to_protofis_warning_tt
			add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_irritation = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_protofis_irritation = 3 }
			}
			set_country_flag = UKR_protofis_stalls_negotiations
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.99 days = 3 } # Bill is killed
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_SHD_influence_flag
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_SHD_meddling_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.13 days = 7 } # Hetman pressures the Soim
			}
			clr_country_flag = UKR_SHD_influence_flag
		}
	}
	option = { # refuse
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.2 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.2.b"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.2.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = 40
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_decrease_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_urdp }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_urdp_support = -10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_protofis }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = 10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_banking_curves_nationalisation_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.3 days = 5 } # Bank crash
				}
				50 = {

				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = ukraine_relief_bill_events.8.t
	desc = ukraine_relief_bill_events.8.d
	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference3
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = UKR_defection_of_independents
	}

	option = { # That's troubling...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.8 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.8.a"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.8.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
}
country_event = { # Protofis suggests to keep selling stockpiled grain
	id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.9
	title = ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.t
	desc = ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.d
	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.14 days = 17 random_days = 4 } # Question of the money reserves
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference3
	option = { # accept
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.9 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.a"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_political_power = 25
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_decrease_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_urdp }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_urdp_support = -10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_protofis }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = 10 }
		}
		country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.10 days = 20 } # New protests. SHD blames the Soim
	}
	option = { # refuse
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.9 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.b"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_urdp }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_urdp_support = 10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_decrease_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_protofis }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = -10 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_promises_to_protofis
			}
			add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_irritation = 1 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_promises_to_protofis_warning_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_protofis_irritation = 3 }
			}
			set_country_flag = UKR_protofis_stalls_negotiations
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.99 days = 3 } # Bill is killed
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # accept ant try to convince others
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.9 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.c"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.9.c
		trigger = { has_political_power > 25 }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = -25
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_decrease_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_urdp }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_urdp_support = -10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_uskhd }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_uskhd_support = 5 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_protofis }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = 10 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_udkhp }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_udkhp_support = 5 }
		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_increase_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_independents }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_independents_support = 10 }
		}
	}
}

				country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.13 days = 7 } # Hetman pressures the Soim
			}

		}

			ideology = social_liberal

		}
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = { localization_key = UKR_relief_bill_support_decrease_slight PARTY = UKR_relief_bill_independents }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_independents_support = -5 }
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

country_event = { # Bill is killed
	id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.99
	title = ukraine_relief_bill_events.99.t
	desc = {
		text = ukraine_relief_bill_events.99.d1
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_defection_of_independents }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukraine_relief_bill_events.99.d2
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_protofis_stalls_negotiations }
	}
	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference3

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.99 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.99.a"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.99.a
		remove_ideas = UKR_black_monday
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_black_monday_recovery
			days = 500
		}
		clear_variable = UKR_BM_length
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = UKR_support_protofis
			}
			add_political_power = -25
		}
		remove_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
		set_country_flag = UKR_bill_failed
		clr_country_flag = UKR_bill_negotiations_flag
		clr_country_flag = UKR_protofis_stalls_negotiations
		clr_country_flag = UKR_defection_of_independents
		clr_country_flag = UKR_SHD_influence_flag
		clear_variable = UKR_independents_support
		clear_variable = UKR_urdp_support
		clear_variable = UKR_protofis_support
		clear_variable = UKR_uskhd_support
		clear_variable = UKR_udkhp_support
		remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_protofis target = THIS }
		remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_URDP target = THIS }
		remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_independents target = THIS }
	}
}
country_event = { # End of the Relief Bill negotiations
	id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.100
	title = ukraine_relief_bill_events.100.t
	desc = ukraine_relief_bill_events.100.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_protofis target = THIS }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_URDP target = THIS }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_independents target = THIS }
			remove_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
			clr_country_flag = UKR_protofis_stalls_negotiations
			clr_country_flag = UKR_defection_of_independents
			clr_country_flag = UKR_SHD_influence_flag
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_doroshenko

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.100 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.100.a"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.100.a # failure
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_bill_success < 4 }
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		remove_ideas = UKR_black_monday
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_black_monday_recovery
			days = 625
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_bill_failed
		clr_country_flag = UKR_bill_negotiations_flag
		clear_variable = UKR_BM_length
		clear_variable = UKR_independents_support
		clear_variable = UKR_urdp_support
		clear_variable = UKR_protofis_support
		clear_variable = UKR_uskhd_support
		clear_variable = UKR_udkhp_support
		clear_variable = UKR_bill_success
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief_bill_events.100 option ukraine_relief_bill_events.100.b"
		name = ukraine_relief_bill_events.100.b #success
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { UKR_bill_success < 4 } }
		}
		remove_ideas = UKR_black_monday
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_black_monday_recovery
			days = UKR_BM_length
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { UKR_bill_success = 4 } } # success
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = UKR_relief_bill_passed
				days = UKR_BM_length
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = { # overwhelming success
				idea = UKR_relief_bill_passed_2
				days = UKR_BM_length
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_bill_successful
		clr_country_flag = UKR_bill_negotiations_flag
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { UKR_protofis_support < 70 } }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_relief_bill_events.101 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_events.34 days = 5 } # Hetman speeks in the Soim
		}
	}
}

	}

		text = ukraine_revolt_events.1.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_towar
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			792 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
			199 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
			GER = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt_events.109 days = 2 } # Event informing about the start of revolt, for GER
			}
			set_variable = { UKR_authdem_foci = 0 }
			set_variable = { UKR_pataut_foci = 0 }
			set_country_flag = UKR_revolt_started #look here
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			country_lock_all_division_template = yes
			set_variable = { UKR_RP_intervention_time = 90 }
			set_variable = { UKR_reinforcement_time = 35 }
			set_variable = { UKR_rebel_attack_time = 14 }
			if = {
				limit = { GAL = { is_ai = no } }
				GAL = { country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt_events.15 days = 12 } }
			}
			else = {
				AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt_events.15 days = 12 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_revolt_events.1 option ukraine_revolt_events.1.a"
		name = ukraine_revolt_events.1.a

			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_REP_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SYNDIE }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_hetman_side_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_side
		complete_national_focus = UKR_flames_of_rebellion
		add_ideas = UKR_anti_hetman_revolt
		set_variable = { UKR_vdr_strength = 25 }
		set_variable = { UKR_pacification_cost = 10 }
		activate_mission = UKR_rebel_attack
		activate_mission = UKR_odessa_in_flames
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt_events.2 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt_events.4 days = 5 } #Rebels secure west
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_bill_successful } }
			add_to_variable = { UKR_vdr_strength = 5 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt_events.52 days = 153 } #If AI can't win revolt by February, autowin it
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_revolt_events.1 option ukraine_revolt_events.1.b"
		name = ukraine_revolt_events.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_USKHD_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_UDKHP_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SHD_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCDEM }

			}

		}

			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt_events.2 days = 1 }

				limit = { is_ai = no }
				random_list = {

					10 = { }

				country_event = { id = ukraine_coalition_events.24 days = 7 }

			country_event = { id = ukraine_land_reform_events.1 days = 46 }

###Land Reform and Industrialisation
country_event = { # Beginning of Land Reform/Industry Mission
	id = ukraine_land_reform_events.1
	title = ukraine_land_reform_events.1.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi } }
		text = ukraine_land_reform_events.1.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi } }
		}
		text = ukraine_land_reform_events.1.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi } }
		text = ukraine_land_reform_events.1.d3
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_farming

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_land_reform_events.1 option ukraine_land_reform_events.1.a"
		name = ukraine_land_reform_events.1.a
		set_country_flag = UKR_land_reform_in_progress
		set_country_flag = UKR_industrialisation_in_progress
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = UKR_landreform_category
		activate_mission = UKR_landreform_mission
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = UKR_industrialisation_category
		activate_mission = UKR_industrialisation_mission
		set_variable = { UKR_reform_in_progress = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_land_reforms_complete = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_industrial_reforms_complete = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_authdem_or_pataut_government = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_shd_events.14 days = 15 }
				country_event = { id = ukraine_lun_events.20 days = 30 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_radicals_may_take_over_natpop_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_radicals_may_take_over_syndicalist_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score > 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_industrialisation_current_tt
		}
	}
}

		name = ukraine_land_reform_events.29.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.005
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.005
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 0.01 }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		}
	}
}

		}

			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_curb_opposition_efforts target = THIS }

			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCDEM }

		}

			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}

					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCLIB }

				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		activate_advisor = UKR_dmytro_doroshenko_sic
	}

	}

	}

			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		complete_national_focus = UKR_the_center_holds
		activate_advisor = UKR_serhii_shemet_sic
		activate_mission = UKR_hetman_scrutiny
		activate_mission = UKR_concerns_among_union
		activate_mission = UKR_scepticism_among_coalition
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = UKR_appoint_loyal_bureaucrats }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = UKR_issue_government_reconstruction_grants }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = UKR_support_viktor_reinbot }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = UKR_drag_down_appointment_procedure }
			country_event = { id = ukraine_coalition_events.31 days = 4 random_days = 2 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_uskhd_promises_tt
		set_variable = { UKR_uskhd_consolidating_variable = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_cant_take_decision_thrice_appoint = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_cant_take_decision_thrice_issue = 0 }
		set_country_flag = UKR_uskhd_consolidating
	}

country_event = { #End to Sickening, Disgusting Evil PARLIAMENTARISM
	id = ukraine_coalition_events.5
	title = ukraine_coalition_events.5.t
	desc = ukraine_coalition_events.5.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_uskhd_symbol
	trigger = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }

	option = { #Parties renamed
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_coalition_events.5 option ukraine_coalition_events.5.a"
		name = ukraine_coalition_events.5.a
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { social_conservative < 0.05 }
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_to_variable = { UKR_uskhd_points = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = UKR_hetman_opposition_party_long
				name = UKR_hetman_opposition_party
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_end_alliance_with_vszv_protofis }
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					long_name = UKR_hetman_opposition_party_long
					name = UKR_hetman_opposition_party
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = UKR_necessary_compromise }
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = market_liberal
					long_name = UKR_hetman_government_party_long
					name = UKR_hetman_government_party
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = UKR_hetman_government_party_long
				name = UKR_hetman_government_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = UKR_hetman_opposition_party_long
				name = UKR_hetman_opposition_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = UKR_hetman_government_party_long
				name = UKR_hetman_government_party
			}
		}
	}
}

								factor = 0
								OR = {
									has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_UDKHP_AUTDEM }
									has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SOCCON }
									has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCLIB }
									has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_HETMANATE_SOCDEM }
								}
							}
							set_country_flag = UKR_uskhd_ai
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ukraine_coalition_events.70

	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_reject_partisanship }
		text = ukraine_coalition_events.70.d2
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_BLR_sojm_meeting

	option = {

				character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi

		}

			limit = { UKR_mykola_mikhnovskyi = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			activate_advisor = UKR_volodymyr_korostovets_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { UKR_volodymyr_korostovets = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			activate_advisor = UKR_mykola_mikhnovskyi_sic
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_coalition_events.70 option ukraine_coalition_events.70.b"
		name = ukraine_coalition_events.70.b #Failure
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_reject_partisanship }
		activate_advisor = UKR_oleksandr_shapoval_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_events.68 days = 365 } #Pavlo Dies, Danylo Succeeds
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Postwar elections
	id = ukraine_coalition_events.73
	title = ukraine_coalition_events.73.t
	desc = ukraine_coalition_events.73.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_election

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_coalition_events.73 option ukraine_coalition_events.73.a"
		name = ukraine_coalition_events.73.a #UDKhP
		trigger = { has_conservative_government = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			}
			activate_advisor = UKR_volodymyr_korostovets_sic
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
				elections_allowed = yes
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.2
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
		else = {
			activate_advisor = UKR_oleksandr_shapoval_sic
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_coalition_events.73 option ukraine_coalition_events.73.b"
		name = ukraine_coalition_events.73.b #Failure
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = DEFAULT } }
			}
		}
		activate_advisor = UKR_viacheslav_prokopovych_sic
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.2
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_coalition_events.73 days = 1460 } #Elections again
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Question of USKhD and UDKhP
	id = ukraine_shd_events.3
	title = ukraine_shd_events.3.t
	desc = ukraine_shd_events.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_hetmanist_symbol
	trigger = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }

	option = { #Fully integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_shd_events.3 option ukraine_shd_events.3.a"
		name = ukraine_shd_events.3.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.06
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_integrate_organisations_full
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = UKR_new_pataut }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
				syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
				radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
				social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
				social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = 0
				paternal_autocrat = UKR_new_pataut
				national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
			country_event = { id = ukraine_shd_events.7 days = 35 }
		}
	}
	option = { #Somewhat integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_shd_events.3 option ukraine_shd_events.3.b"
		name = ukraine_shd_events.3.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_stability = -0.03
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_integrate_organisations_half
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { UKR_new_authdem = UKR.party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
			divide_temp_variable = { UKR_new_authdem = 2 }

			set_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = UKR.party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = UKR_new_authdem }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = UKR_new_authdem }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = UKR_new_pataut }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
				syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
				radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
				social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
				social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = UKR_new_authdem
				paternal_autocrat = UKR_new_pataut
				national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
			country_event = { id = ukraine_shd_events.7 days = 35 }
		}
	}
	option = { #Don't integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_shd_events.3 option ukraine_shd_events.3.c"
		name = ukraine_shd_events.3.c
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

	id = ukraine_shd_events.24
	title = ukraine_shd_events.24.t
	desc = ukraine_shd_events.24.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_cossacks

	trigger = {
		has_government = paternal_autocrat
		has_war_with = RUS
		any_owned_state = {
			has_state_flag = UKR_cossack_militia_empowered
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_shd_events.24 option ukraine_shd_events.24.a"
		name = ukraine_shd_events.24.a
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Cossack Militia Division"
				LINE_1 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = cavalry ICON = GFX_unit_cavalry_icon_small COUNT = 9 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Cossack Militia Division" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Cossack Militia Division" disband = yes } #no cheating
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Cossack Militia Division"
				division_names_group = UKR_INF_01
				regiments = {
					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					cavalry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					cavalry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					cavalry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					cavalry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				}
				priority = 2
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			display_individual_scopes = yes
			limit = { has_state_flag = UKR_cossack_militia_empowered }
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_spawn_unit
					TYPE = "Cossack Militia Division"
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Cossack Militia Division\" start_experience_factor = 0.35"
					owner = ROOT
				}
			}
			clr_state_flag = UKR_cossack_militia_empowered
		}
	}
}

			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_radical_pop = UKR_socdem_pop }
					check_variable = { UKR_radical_pop = UKR_socialist_pop }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_socdem_pop = UKR_socialist_pop }
					check_variable = { UKR_socdem_pop > UKR_radical_pop }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ukraine_republican_events.10.e.tt
		add_stability = -0.1

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = UKR_opanas_fedenko_sic

		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = ukraine_republican_events.10.tt

		hidden_effect = {
			UKR_isaak_mazepa = { promote_character = social_democrat_subtype }
			complete_national_focus = UKR_solidarity_and_compromise
		}
	}
	option = { #Election tie - SocDem/RadSoc coalition
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.10 option ukraine_republican_events.10.g"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.10.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_radical_pop = UKR_socdem_pop }
					check_variable = { UKR_radical_pop = UKR_socialist_pop }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_radical_pop = UKR_socialist_pop }
					check_variable = { UKR_radical_pop > UKR_socdem_pop }
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_socdem_pop = UKR_socialist_pop }
					check_variable = { UKR_socdem_pop > UKR_radical_pop }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ukraine_republican_events.10.e.tt
		add_stability = -0.1
		country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.13 days = 1 } #Forming the New Government
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_landreform_election_promises_flag }
			activate_mission = UKR_landreform_election_promises
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_industry_election_promises_flag }
			activate_mission = UKR_industry_election_promises
		}
		clr_country_flag = UKR_elections_in_progress
	}
}

			remove_targeted_decision = { target = BLR decision = UKR_fund_bdsp }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = BLR decision = UKR_launch_coup_belarus }
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_revbloc_collapse

			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_socialist_nationalization }

	fire_only_once = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = UKR_social_democrat_no_usb_long
				name = UKR_social_democrat_no_usb
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.131 option ukraine_republican_events.131.a"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.131.a
		add_ideas = UKR_minority_government
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
			UKR_isaak_mazepa = { promote_character = social_democrat_subtype }
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = UKR_opanas_fedenko_sic
		deactivate_advisor = UKR_arnold_margolin_unremovable_advisor
		set_can_be_fired_in_advisor_role = {
			character = UKR_arnold_margolin
			value = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			UKR_clear_revbloc_ideas = yes
			complete_national_focus = UKR_solidarity_and_compromise
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = UKR_fight_and_you_will_overcome
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = POL decision = UKR_fund_polish_socialists }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = BLR decision = UKR_fund_bdsp }
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = BLR decision = UKR_launch_coup_belarus }
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_revbloc_collapse
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_socialist_nationalization }
			clr_country_flag = UKR_socialist_nationalization
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_remove_socialist_nationalization
		}
	}
}

				add_idea = UKR_GER_deal_2
			}
		}

			limit = { has_idea = UKR_GER_deal_2 }

			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { UKR_radicalism_score = 2 }
		UKR_radicalism_change = yes

		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_socialisation_no_buff_tt
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.135 days = 3 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #Military Spending Debate
	id = ukraine_republican_events.163
	title = ukraine_republican_events.163.t
	desc = ukraine_republican_events.163.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_BLR_sojm_meeting

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.163 option ukraine_republican_events.163.a"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.163.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_national_defence_act_var < 3 }
			}
			country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.164 days = 1 } #Failure
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_national_defence_act_var = 3 }
			}
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.164 days = 1 } #Failure
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.165 days = 1 } #Success
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_national_defence_act_var = 4 }
			}
			random_list = {
				60 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.164 days = 1 } #Failure
				}
				40 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.165 days = 1 } #Success
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_national_defence_act_var = 5 }
			}
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.164 days = 1 } #Failure
				}
				60 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.165 days = 1 } #Success
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_national_defence_act_var = 6 }
			}
			random_list = {
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.164 days = 1 } #Failure
				}
				80 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.165 days = 1 } #Success
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_national_defence_act_var = 7 }
			}
			country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.165 days = 1 } #Success
		}
	}
}

			limit = { has_government = social_liberal }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = ukraine_republican_events.174.a.tt
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			set_variable = { UKR_usdrp_idealism_points = 0 }
			remove_mission = UKR_scepticism_within_the_party
			remove_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = UKR_emphasise_commitment_to_principles }
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = ukraine_republican_events.174.a2.tt
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_coalition_partner_uncooperative }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_coalition_partner_indifferent }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_coalition_partner_cooperative }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_coalition_partner_amenable }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Postwar Election Results - USDRP
	id = ukraine_republican_events.229
	title = ukraine_republican_events.229.t
	desc = ukraine_republican_events.229.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_election
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			hold_election = ROOT
			country_event = { id = ukraine_republican_events.75 days = 1460 } #Next elections
			country_event = { id = ukraine_events.84 days = 45 }
		}
	}

	option = { #Major failure
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.229 option ukraine_republican_events.229.a"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.229.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_election_var < 3 }
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_major_failure
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		activate_advisor = UKR_viacheslav_prokopovych_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.2
		}
	}
	option = { #Minor failure
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.229 option ukraine_republican_events.229.b"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.229.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_election_var = 3 }
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_minor_failure
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		activate_advisor = UKR_viacheslav_prokopovych_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.1
		}
	}
	option = { #Mazepa
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.229 option ukraine_republican_events.229.c"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.229.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = { UKR_election_var > 3 }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_major_victory } }
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_country_flag = UKR_petliura_hired
								UKR_symon_petliura = {
									is_unit_leader = yes
									skill > 3
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					is_ai = yes
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_REP_SOCDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = UKR_ivan_romanchenko_sic
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_major_victory }
			}
			set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_minor_victory
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = UKR_social_democrat_upsr_usdrp_long
				name = UKR_social_democrat_upsr_usdrp
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_major_victory
				country_event = ukraine_republican_events.259
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Fedenko
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.229 option ukraine_republican_events.229.e"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.229.e
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_election_var > 3 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_major_victory } }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = UKR_petliura_hired
						UKR_symon_petliura = {
							is_unit_leader = yes
							skill > 3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		UKR_opanas_fedenko = { promote_character = social_democrat_subtype }
		activate_advisor = UKR_ivan_romanchenko_sic
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_major_victory }
			}
			set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_minor_victory
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = UKR_social_democrat_upsr_usdrp_long
				name = UKR_social_democrat_upsr_usdrp
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_major_victory
				country_event = ukraine_republican_events.259
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Petliura
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.229 option ukraine_republican_events.229.f"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.229.f
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_election_var > 3 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_major_victory }
				}
				has_country_flag = UKR_petliura_hired
				UKR_symon_petliura = {
					is_unit_leader = yes
					skill > 3
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		UKR_symon_petliura = { promote_character = social_democrat_subtype }
		clr_country_flag = UKR_petliura_hired

		activate_advisor = UKR_ivan_romanchenko_sic
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = UKR_major_victory }
			}
			set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_minor_victory
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = UKR_usdrp_major_victory
				country_event = ukraine_republican_events.259
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Major success - Kovalevskyi
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican_events.229 option ukraine_republican_events.229.g"
		name = ukraine_republican_events.229.g

				long_name = UKR_market_liberal_party_long2
				name = UKR_market_liberal_party2
			}
			UKR_oleksandr_shulhyn = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
					promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
				}
				else = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							desc = UKR_oleksandr_shulhyn_leader_desc
							ideology = market_liberal_subtype
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = UKR_triumph_of_the_national_revolution
		set_politics = { ruling_party = national_populist elections_allowed = no }
		add_ideas = UKR_lun_resistance1
		retire_character = UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi
		clr_country_flag = UKR_SHD_tree
		clr_country_flag = UKR_authdem_tree
		set_country_flag = UKR_LUN_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_variable = { UKR_lun_mechanic_stability = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_lun_mechanic_political_power = 0 }
		set_variable = { UKR_lun_mechanic_factory_output = 0 }
		force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		set_variable = {
			UKR_lun_mechanic_variable = 3
			tooltip = UKR_lun_mechanic_enable_tt
		}

		remove_mission = UKR_industrialisation_mission
		remove_mission = UKR_landreform_mission
		clr_country_flag = UKR_land_reform_in_progress

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_debacle }

				add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {

			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_1 }
				swap_ideas = {

					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_2
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_3
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_2
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { UKR_land_reform_score < 30 } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_1
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_2
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_3
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_3
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { UKR_land_reform_score < 40 } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_1
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_4

					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_2
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_3 }

					remove_idea = UKR_land_reform_wip_3
					add_idea = UKR_failed_land_reform_4

			}
		}

				}

country_event = { # Bloc lets Borotbists into Parliament, They jointly dissolve it
	id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.20
	title = ukraine_borotbyst_events.20.t
	desc = ukraine_borotbyst_events.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_oleksandr_shumskyi
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_borotbyst_events.20 option ukraine_borotbyst_events.20.a"
		name = ukraine_borotbyst_events.20.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		UKR_symon_petliura = { retire = yes }
		UKR_mykhailo_omelianovych_pavlenko = { retire = yes }
		UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi = { retire = yes }
		UKR_oleksandr_udovychenko = { retire = yes }
		UKR_omelian_volokh = { promote_leader = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		activate_advisor = UKR_mykhailo_poloz_sic
		remove_ideas = UKR_syndie_general_strike
		remove_ideas = UKR_confused_army
		leave_faction = yes
		MIE_remove_from_intermarium = yes
		UKR_update_military = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_military_access_to = UKR
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = PREV
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_borotbysts_ukapist_bakhmut_pact
			}
			add_ideas = UKR_shaky_cooperation
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.72 days = 6 }
			}
		}
		UKR_syndie_revolution_angry_constitution = yes
		UKR_clear_republic_ideas = yes
		complete_national_focus = UKR_fighters_til_the_end
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_borotbyst_popularity_mechanic_tt
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus = UKR.party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_bakhmut_meeting_agree_to_ukapist
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus = UKR.party_popularity_100@totalist }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus > 30 }
				has_country_flag = UKR_bakhmut_meeting_agree_to_ukapist
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_popular_revolution_tt
			add_ideas = UKR_revolutionary_might
			add_ideas = UKR_petliurites5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus > 14 }
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = UKR_bakhmut_meeting_agree_to_ukapist
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_medium_popular_revolution_tt
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = UKR_petliurites3
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_unpopular_revolution_tt
			add_ideas = UKR_unpopular_revolution
			add_ideas = UKR_petliurites1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_economic_standstill
			days = 365
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_economic_crisis_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_leave_mitteleuropa = yes
			GER = { end_puppet = UKR }
			set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_republic
			country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.21 days = 3 }
			if = { #White Russia not at war with Germany
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
					}
				}
				GER = { country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.100 days = 5 } } #Decision to attack Ukraine
				RUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.100 days = 5 } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							owns_state = 89 #Stanislawow
							owns_state = 91 #Lwow
						}
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.100 days = 5 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = { #Red Russia not at war with Germany
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_socialist_government = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
					}
				}
				GER = { country_event = { id = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.32 days = 5 } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							owns_state = 89 #Stanislawow
							owns_state = 91 #Lwow
						}
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.32 days = 5 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = { #White Russia at war with Germany
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_socialist_government = no
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = UKR
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = RUS }
					}
					white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
				}
				GER = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = UKR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							owns_state = 89 #Stanislawow
							owns_state = 91 #Lwow
						}
						NOT = { has_war_with = AUS }
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.32 days = 5 } }
				}
				add_ideas = UKR_fighters_till_the_end
			}
			else_if = { #Red Russia at war with Germany
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_socialist_government = yes
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = UKR
					}
					white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
				}
				GER = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = UKR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							owns_state = 89 #Stanislawow
							owns_state = 91 #Lwow
						}
						NOT = { has_war_with = AUS }
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.32 days = 5 } }
				}
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.73 days = 3 }
			news_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.200 days = 1 }
		}
	}

				country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.70 days = 30 }

			}
		}
	}

		add_stability = -0.02

		}

			exists = yes

			is_subject = no
		}

			}

				any_neighbor_country = { is_in_faction_with = INT }
			}
		}
	}

		days = 7
	}

	option = { #Offer peace to RUS, inform UKR

	title = ukraine_borotbyst_events.115.t
	desc = ukraine_borotbyst_events.115.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		has_socialist_government = yes
		is_subject = no
		RUS = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			surrender_progress < 0.1
		}
		NOT = {
			is_neighbor_of = INT
			AND = {
				NOT = { country_exists = GER }
				any_neighbor_country = { is_in_faction_with = INT }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_borotbyst_events.115 option ukraine_borotbyst_events.115.a"
		name = ukraine_borotbyst_events.115.a

			country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbyst_events.116 days = 60 random_days = 20 }
		}
		UKR_update_military = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = syndicalist }
			activate_advisor = UKR_andrii_khvylia_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = radical_socialist }
			activate_advisor = UKR_volodymyr_chekhivskyi_sic
		}
		get_current_government_type = yes
		RUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = UKR
				autonomy_state = autonomous_puppet
				end_wars = no
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 7 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		remove_ideas = UKR_economic_standstill
		227 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		228 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}

		trigger = { UKR = { has_government = national_populist } }
		text = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15.lun.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { UKR = { has_government = social_democrat } }
		text = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15.unr.b
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15 option ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15.a"
		name = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					AND = {
						UKR = { has_government = national_populist }
						GER = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						UKR = { has_government = social_democrat }
						GER = { has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				UKR = { has_government = social_democrat }
				BLR = { has_government = social_democrat }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -15
		UKR = { country_event = { id = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.16 days = 2 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15 option ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15.b"
		name = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.15.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		UKR = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.17 days = 2 }
			set_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #GER-UKR deal
	id = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25
	title = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25.t
	desc = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25 option ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25.a"
		name = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25.a
		trigger = { tag = UKR }
		if = {
			limit = { has_autonomy_state = oststaat }
			MIE_promote_oststaat = yes
		}
		GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = german_research
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_compromise } #Most lenient deal
			add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh } #Strictest deal
			add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_3
			add_to_variable = { UKR_landreform_cost = 15 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_increase_reform_cost_15
		}
		else = { #Moderate deal
			add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_2
			add_to_variable = { UKR_landreform_cost = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_increase_reform_cost_10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			set_country_flag = illusion_of_free_choice_achievement_condition
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25 option ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25.a"
		name = ukraine_foreign_policy_events.25.a
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_soclib_or_socdem_government = yes
					UKR = { has_government = national_populist }
				}
				country_event = { id = germany_foreign_events_new.83 days = 20 random_days = 10 }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			UKR = {
				GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = german_research
				GER = { add_to_faction = UKR }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_compromise } #Most lenient deal
					add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_1
					add_political_power = -5
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh } #Strictest deal
					add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_3
					add_political_power = 40
				}
				else = { #Moderate deal
					add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_2
					add_political_power = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden AI event for going radical paths
	id = ukraine_events.1000

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = { #LUN coup will not happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.1000 option 1"
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_NATPOP }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #LUN coup will happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.1000 option 2"
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_NATPOP } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_ai_lun_coup
	}
	option = { #Borotbyst revolution will not happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.1000 option 3"
		trigger = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = UKR_republic
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SYNDIE }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Borotbyst revolution will happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_events.1000 option 4"
		trigger = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = UKR_republic
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SYNDIE } }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_ai_borotbyst_revolution
	}
}
